\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Internal function for adding a flag \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{详细描述}
Creates a command line program, with very few defaults. 

To use, create a new {\ttfamily Program()} instance with {\ttfamily argc}, {\ttfamily argv}, and a help description. The templated add\+\_\+option methods make it easy to prepare options. Remember to call {\ttfamily .start} before starting your program, so that the options can be evaluated and the help option doesn\textquotesingle{}t accidentally run your program.

Parse a short (false) or long (true) argument, must be at the top of the list if local\+\_\+processing\+\_\+only is set to true then fallthrough is disabled will return false if not found return true if the argument was processed or false if nothing was done if we require a separator add it here函数调用图\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_c_l_i_1_1_app_abdca3e2d9d0fbcc86a353e832285e509} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_c_l_i11_8hpp_ae98448e41749e6ca61eebe5c743a2a01}{CLI11\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} CLI\+::\+App\+::\+\_\+parse\+\_\+positional (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::vector$<$ std\+::string $>$ \&}]{args}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{halt\+On\+Subcommand}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Parse a positional, go up the tree to check 
\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em halt\+On\+Subcommand} & if set to true the operation will not process subcommands merely return false Return true if the positional was used false otherwise \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Try to find a local subcommand that is repeated

now try one last gasp at subcommands that have been executed before, go to root app and try to find a subcommand in a broader way, if one exists let the parent deal with it

If this is an option group don\textquotesingle{}t deal with it

We are out of other options this goes to missing函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{class_c_l_i_1_1_app_adb68306d25a26400399d11efe7211dc4}\index{CLI::App@{CLI::App}!add\_option@{add\_option}}
\index{add\_option@{add\_option}!CLI::App@{CLI::App}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{add\_option()}{add\_option()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_c_l_i_1_1_app_adb68306d25a26400399d11efe7211dc4} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_c_l_i11_8hpp_ae98448e41749e6ca61eebe5c743a2a01}{CLI11\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c_l_i_1_1_option}{Option}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} CLI\+::\+App\+::add\+\_\+option (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::string}]{option\+\_\+name}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_c_l_i_aee5516e2fe4d7b0298d5491d73ccefe5}{callback\+\_\+t}}}]{option\+\_\+callback}{, }\item[{std\+::string}]{option\+\_\+description}{ = {\ttfamily "{}"{}}, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{defaulted}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}}}, }\item[{std\+::function$<$ std\+::string()$>$}]{func}{ = {\ttfamily \{\}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Add an option, will automatically understand the type for common types.

To use, create a variable with the expected type, and pass it in after the name. After start is called, you can use count to see if the value was passed, and the value will be initialized properly. \doxylink{example__custom__name_8cpp_a2c973620a3fe7f923747ed2baa1bae4e}{Numbers}, vectors, and strings are supported.

-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{test__tbb__version_8cpp_a24f5b267393bc143788c08f4641a1830a4f6fc19321f5eedb3b03f420dfa7244c}{required()}, -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}default, and the validators are options, The positional options take an optional number of arguments.

For example, \begin{DoxyVerb}std::string filename;
program.add_option("filename", filename, "description of filename");
\end{DoxyVerb}

\Hypertarget{class_c_l_i_1_1_app_af51ab8b76ecf5404a4ff442cec071d55}\index{CLI::App@{CLI::App}!callback@{callback}}
\index{callback@{callback}!CLI::App@{CLI::App}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{callback()}{callback()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_c_l_i_1_1_app_af51ab8b76ecf5404a4ff442cec071d55} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_c_l_i_1_1_app}{App}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} CLI\+::\+App\+::callback (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::function$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}}()$>$}]{app\+\_\+callback}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Set a callback for execution when all parsing and processing has completed

Due to a bug in c++11, it is not possible to overload on std\+::function (fixed in c++14 and backported to c++11 on newer compilers). Use capture by reference to get a pointer to \doxylink{class_c_l_i_1_1_app}{App} if needed. 函数调用图\+:
